bit of wordplay here; in high school, Frank wasn’t considered a “tough guy” but he could show a rougher side, conveyed through the &lt;strong&gt;opposition&lt;/strong&gt; used here with “soft and &lt;a href=\&quot;http://www.thefreedictionary.com/jagged\&quot; rel=\&quot;noopener nofollow\&quot;&gt;“jagged”&lt;/a&gt;. There’s a wordplay on \&quot;jagged” and “jacket” here, i.e. the letter jackets worn by high school jocks. “Jagged” could also refer to his sexual orientation with the idea that he’s not straight. Also, in reference to the last line, “jagged” is the opposite of straight-edge.&lt;/p&gt;\n\n&lt;p&gt;Essentially, Frank insulted one of the other jocks and the guy got upset. Also, in reference to the last line, “jagged” is the opposite of straight-edge.\n\nEssentially, Frank insulted one of the other jocks and the guy got upset.       <div class="annotation_label">
        
          <h3 class="u-inline">
            About “Sunday”
          </h3>
        
        
      </div>
      <div class="rich_text_formatting">
        <p>Earl and <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Frank-ocean" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/artists/1985">Frank Ocean</a> have also collaborated together on Frank Ocean’s <a href="https://genius.com/Frank-ocean-super-rich-kids-lyrics" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/songs/78960">“Super Rich Kids”</a> off of his 2013 album <em>Channel Orange</em>. Here, the two Odd Future members reflect on sour relationships, drug use, and their lives in Los Angeles over a mellow beat, co-produced by both of them.</p>

<p><img src="https://images.rapgenius.com/1024ab3113e92dad99960747a6e18004.554x614x1.jpg" alt="" width="554" height="614" data-animated="false"></p>
      </div>
      <div class="song_metadata u-xx_large_bottom_margin"></div>
    </div>
